#### 2. Filtering Basics: HTTP

###### Set A

- Command to show only the HTTP traffic from a PCAP file?

```sh
student@attackdefense:~$ tshark -Y 'http' -r HTTP_traffic.pcap
   30   4.166998 192.168.252.128 → 54.239.32.8  HTTP 904 GET / HTTP/1.1
   38   4.168852 192.168.252.128 → 54.239.39.114 HTTP 1150 POST /1/batch/1/OE/ HTTP/1.1  (text/plain)
   46   4.472330 54.239.39.114 → 192.168.252.128 HTTP 431 HTTP/1.1 204 No Content  146   5.060440 192.168.252.128 → 52.84.108.225 HTTP 399 GET /images/I/412maSA0fuL._AC_SY200_.jpg HTTP/1.1  150   5.062201 192.168.252.128 → 52.84.108.225 HTTP 399 GET /images/I/41wuVnAeedL._AC_SY200_.jpg HTTP/1.1  158   5.068393 192.168.252.128 → 52.84.108.225 HTTP 399 GET /images/I/412OwlOMxPL._AC_SY200_.jpg HTTP/1.1

  162   5.068562 192.168.252.128 → 52.84.108.225 HTTP 399 GET /images/I/41O1oRMP6pL._AC_SY200_.jpg HTTP/1.1
```

- Command to print only packets only source IP and URL for all GET request packets?


```sh
student@attackdefense:~$ tshark -Y 'http.request.method==GET' -Tfields -e ip.src -e http.request.full_uri -r HTTP_traffic.pcap
```

###### Set B

- How many HTTP packets contain the "password" string?

```sh
student@attackdefense:~$ tshark -r HTTP_traffic.pcap -Y "http contains password"12866  99.041118 52.84.108.101 ? 192.168.252.128 HTTP 1573 HTTP/1.1 200 OK  (text/javascript)13089  99.686253 52.84.108.101 ? 192.168.252.128 HTTP 7905 HTTP/1.1 200 OK  (text/css)
13173 100.072333 52.84.108.101 ? 192.168.252.128 HTTP 12836 HTTP/1.1 200 OK  (text/javascript)13185 100.077752 52.84.108.101 ? 192.168.252.128 HTTP 5527 HTTP/1.1 200 OK  (text/javascript)student@attackdefense:~$
```

----

- Which IP address was sent GET requests for New York Times (www.nytimes.com)?

```sh
student@attackdefense:~$ tshark -r HTTP_traffic.pcap -Y "http.request.method==GET && http.host==www.nytimes.com" -Tfields -e ip.dst
170.149.159.130
student@attackdefense:~$
```
